\index{invoke\_with\_signal\_handler@{invoke\_with\_signal\_handler}!sysio::vm@{sysio::vm}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{invoke\_with\_signal\_handler()}{invoke\_with\_signal\_handler()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacesysio_1_1vm_a071298ad9404d4cd62434edde161b767} 
template$<$typename F , typename E $>$ \\
auto sysio\+::vm\+::invoke\+\_\+with\+\_\+signal\+\_\+handler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{F \&\&}]{f}{, }\item[{E \&\&}]{e}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\doxylink{struct_call}{Call} a function with a signal handler installed. If this thread is signalled during the execution of f, the function e will be called with the signal number as an argument. If f creates any automatic variables with non-\/trivial destructors, then it must mask the relevant signals during the lifetime of these objects or the behavior is undefined.

signals handled\+: SIGSEGV, SIGBUS, SIGFPE 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sysio_2vm_2signals_8hpp_source_l00123}{123}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sysio_2vm_2signals_8hpp_source}{signals.\+hpp}}.
